    function getCurrentCart() {
      let cart = {};
      $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: "/cart.js",
        dataType: "json",
        async: false,
        success: function(cartResp) {
          cart = cartResp;
        }
      });

      return cart;
    }
  
    function addProductsToCart(cart) {
    let isSuccess = false;
    internalCall = true
    for (var key in cart.items) {
      var item = cart.items[key];
      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/cart/add.js",
        dataType: "json",
        async: false,
        data: {
          quantity: item.quantity, 
          id: item.shopifyProductVariantReference,
          bolt: true,
        },
        success: function() {
          isSuccess = true;
        }
      });
    }
    return isSuccess;
  	}


    // Synchronous calls to clear the cart
    function clearCart() {
      let isSuccess = false;
      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/cart/clear.js",
        dataType: "json",
        async: false,
        success: function() {
          isSuccess = true;
        }
      });

      return isSuccess;
    }
    
     var trackGaStepProduct = function(step) {
      if (!enableGaTrackingProduct) {
        return;
      }
      ga('ec:setAction','checkout', {
        'step': step,
      });
      ga('send', 'event', 'Checkout', 'step');
    };
    
    
      var pollForShopifyOrderUrlProduct = function(transaction, callback) {
        var url = window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.host + 
            "/apps/boltapp/v1/shopify/order/confirmation?order_token=" + orderTokenProduct +
            "&reference=" + referenceProduct +
            "&format=json";
        var MaxRetryCount = 10;
        var currentRetryCount = 0;
        var cart = "";
        var orderUrlFunc = function(){
          $.ajax({
            url: url,
            success: function(result) {
              successUrlProduct = (result && result.cart && result.cart.merchant_order_url) || "";
              console.log(result.cart);
            },
            complete: function(data){
              currentRetryCount = currentRetryCount + 1;
              if (successUrlProduct === "") {
                if (currentRetryCount <= MaxRetryCount) {
                  window.setTimeout(orderUrlFunc, 2000);
                } else {
                  callback();
                  console.log("time out after " + MaxRetryCount + "attempts");
                }
              } else {
                console.log("retrieving shopify order_number for " + successUrlProduct);
                callback();
              }
            }
          });
        };
        window.setTimeout(orderUrlFunc, 2000);
    }
    
    function logErrorProduct(err) {
      console.error(err.message, err.exception);
      if (window.boltBugsnagClient) {
        window.boltBugsnagClient.leaveBreadcrumb(err.message);
        window.boltBugsnagClient.notify(err.exception);
      } else {
        console.error("bugsnag is not setup");
      }
    }

    function truncProduct(x) {
      // Math.truncProduct does not exist in IE
      if (Math.truncProduct) {
        return Math.truncProduct(x);
      } else {
        var n = x - x%1;
        return n===0 && (x<0 || (x===0 && (1/x !== 1/0))) ? -0 : n;
      };
    }
    
      var inventoryChecksRemainingProduct = 0;
      var orderValidationProduct = function(callback) {
        console.log("ORDERVALIDATION");
        var inventoryCheckCallbackProduct = function(success, product) {
          var response = {
            success: success,
            errorMessage: !success && product ? product + " is out of stock." : null,
          };
          callback(response);
        }

        // This event is triggered after the checkout form is loaded, cart response will be present.
        inventoryChecksRemainingProduct = 1;
        productInventoryCheckProduct(globalBoltCart.items[0], inventoryCheckCallbackProduct);
      }
      
        function productInventoryCheckProduct(item, inventoryCheckCallbackProduct) {
        console.log("INVENTORY CHECKED");
        $.ajax({
          type: "GET",
          url: "/products/" + item.handle + ".json",
          dataType: "json",
          success: function(response) {
            var product = response.product;
            var variants = product.variants;
            var variant = null;

            for (var i = 0; i < variants.length; i++) {
              if (variants[i].id === item.variant_id) {
                variant = variants[i];
                break;
              }
            }

            if (variant == null) {
              inventoryCheckCallbackProduct(false, item.title);
              return;
            }

            var isShopifyManagement = variant.inventory_management === "shopify";
            var isInventoryEnforced =  variant.inventory_policy === "deny";
            var insufficientQuantity = variant.inventory_quantity < item.quantity;
            var denyPurchase = isShopifyManagement && isInventoryEnforced && insufficientQuantity;

            if (denyPurchase) {
              inventoryCheckCallbackProduct(false, item.title);
            } else {
              inventoryChecksRemainingProduct--;

              if (inventoryChecksRemainingProduct == 0) {
                inventoryCheckCallbackProduct(true, null);
              }
            }
          },
          error: function(xhr, status, errorThrown) {
            inventoryCheckCallbackProduct(false, item.title);
            logErrorProduct({message: 'Error running product inventory check', exception: errorThrown});
          }
        });
      }
    
    

    // AJAX call to get all the shipping options for the current cart
    function getShippingOptionsProduct(event, eventData, origin) {
      var partialURL = "/cart/shipping_rates.json?";
      var postalCodeParam = "shipping_address%5Bzip%5D=" + encodeURIComponent(eventData.address.postal_code);
      var countryCodeParam = "shipping_address%5Bcountry%5D=" + encodeURIComponent(eventData.address.country_code);
      var provinceCodeParam = "shipping_address%5Bprovince%5D=" + encodeURIComponent(eventData.address.region);
      var fullURL = partialURL + "&" + postalCodeParam + "&" + countryCodeParam + "&" + provinceCodeParam;

      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: fullURL,
        dataType: "json",
        error: function(xhr, textStatus, errorThrown) {
          var response = {
            type: "fetched_shopify_shipping",
            error: true,
          };
          event.source.postMessage(JSON.stringify(response), origin);
        },
        success: function(shippingOptionsResponse) {
          var boltShippingOptions = [];
          var i = 0;
          var defaultCurrency = "USD";
          var defaultCurrencySymbol = "$";
          for (; i < shippingOptionsResponse.shipping_rates.length; i++) {
            var boltShippingOption = {};
            boltShippingOption.service = shippingOptionsResponse.shipping_rates[i].name;
            boltShippingOption.cost = {};
            boltShippingOption.cost.currency = shippingOptionsResponse.shipping_rates[i].currency || defaultCurrency;
            boltShippingOption.cost.amount = truncProduct(parseFloat(shippingOptionsResponse.shipping_rates[i].price)  * 100);
            boltShippingOption.cost.currency_symbol = currencySymbolByISOCurrencyCode[shippingOptionsResponse.shipping_rates[i].currency] || defaultCurrencySymbol;
            boltShippingOptions.push(boltShippingOption);
            if (boltShippingOption.cost.currency) {
              defaultCurrency = boltShippingOption.cost.currency;
            }
            if (boltShippingOption.cost.currency_symbol) {
              defaultCurrencySymbol = boltShippingOption.cost.currency_symbol;
            }
          }
          var response = {
            type: "fetched_shopify_shipping",
            shipping_options: boltShippingOptions,
            address: eventData.address,
          };
          event.source.postMessage(JSON.stringify(response), origin);
        }
      });
    }

    function receiveMessageProduct(event) {
      if (!event) {
        return;
      }

      var origin = event.origin || event.originalEvent.origin;
      if (expectedOrigins.indexOf(origin) < 0 || !event.data) {
        return;
      }

      var eventData;
      try {
        eventData = JSON.parse(event.data);
      } catch (e) {
        return;
      }

      if (eventData && eventData.type === 'bolt_order_token') {
        orderTokenProduct = eventData.token;
        return;
      }

      if (!eventData || eventData.type !== 'fetch_shopify_shipping') {
        return;
      }
//         var currentCart = getCurrentCart();
//         var itemIncludedInCart = false;
//         for (var i = 0; i < currentCart.items.length; i++) {
//           if (currentCart.items[i].variant_id === variantID) {
//             itemIncludedInCart = true;
//             break;
//           }
//         }
//         if (!itemIncludedInCart) {
//           addProductsToCart(globalBoltCart);
//         }
      console.log("SHIPPING");
      console.log(getCurrentCart());
      getShippingOptionsProduct(event, eventData, origin);
    }

    async function configureCheckout() {
      var sub = BoltConnect.configureProductCheckout(
        globalBoltCart,
        {},
        {
          check: function() {
            console.log("HEREEEEEEEE");
            trackGaStepProduct(1);
            clearCart();
            globalBoltCart.items[0].quantity = parseInt($('input#Quantity-product-template').val());
      		addProductsToCart(globalBoltCart);
            inBoltCheckout = true;
          	return true;
          },
          onCheckoutStart: function() {
            console.log("Checkout started");
            trackGaStepProduct(2);
            if (enableFacebookPixelProduct) {
            	fbq('track', 'InitiateCheckout');
          	}
          },
          onShippingDetailsComplete: function() {
          	trackGaStepProduct(3);
          },
          onShippingOptionsComplete: function() {
          	trackGaStepProduct(4);
          },
          onPaymentSubmit: function() {
          	trackGaStepProduct(5);
          	if (enableFacebookPixelProduct) {
            	fbq('track', 'AddPaymentInfo');
          	}
          },
          success: function(transaction, callback) {
            clearCart();
            addProductsToCart(previousCart);
            referenceProduct = transaction.reference;
            if (shopifyConfirmationRendererProduct) {
            	pollForShopifyOrderUrlProduct(transaction, callback);
            } else {
                callback();
            }
            if (enableGaTrackingProduct) {
              ga('ec:setAction', 'purchase', {     
                'id': transaction.reference,                     
                'revenue': String(transaction.amount.amount / 100.0)              
              });
              ga('send', 'event');
              trackGaStepProduct(6);
            }
            if (enableFacebookPixelProduct) {
              fbq('track', 'Purchase', {
                value: transaction.amount.amount / 100,
                currency: 'USD',
              });
            }
          },
          close: function() {
            inBoltCheckout = false;
            try {
              if (successUrlProduct != "") {
              	window.location = successUrlProduct;
              }
              else if (orderTokenProduct && referenceProduct) {
              	window.location = "/apps/boltapp/v1/shopify/order/confirmation?order_token=" + orderTokenProduct + "&reference=" + referenceProduct;
              } else {
                console.log("ONCLOSE")
                console.log(previousCart);
        	    clearCart();
                addProductsToCart(previousCart);
              }
            } catch (e) {
              logErrorProduct({message: 'An exception occurred redirecting', exception: e});
            }
          },
//           orderValidation: orderValidationProduct
        },
        {
  		  checkoutButtonClassName: "bolt-checkout-button-product",
		},
      );
    }
     
    // Loads the current product details
    function loadProductPageCheckoutCart() {
      var boltCart = {
        "authcapture": autoCapture,
      };
      $.ajax({
        type: "GET",

          if (optionsSelectedIndex == -1) {
            for (x=0; x<parsedProduct.variants.length; x++) {      
              if (parsedProduct.variants[x].id == 31825568071734) {
        		optionsSelectedIndex = x;
        		break;
              }
            }
          }
          var propertiesBolt = []
          for (var key in parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].properties) {
             if (properties.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                propertiesBolt.push({ name: key, value: properties[key] });
             }
          }
          boltCart.items = [{
            image: parsedProduct.image && parsedProduct.image.src,
            desc: parsedProduct.body_html,
            name: parsedProduct.title + ' ' + parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].title,
            reference: parsedProduct.id + ':' + parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].id,
            shopifyProductVariantReference: parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].id,
            shopifyProductReference: parsedProduct.id,
            quantity: parseInt($('input#Quantity-product-template').val()),
            sku: parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].sku,
            price: "$" + parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].price,
            options: parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].title,
            taxable: parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].taxable,
            properties: propertiesBolt,
          }];

          productID = parsedProduct.id;
          variantID = parsedProduct.variants[optionsSelectedIndex].id;
          boltCart.currency = {
            "currency_code": "USD",
            "currency_symbol": "$"
          };
             
          globalBoltCart = boltCart;
          configureCheckout();
        }
      });
    }

    window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessageProduct, false);
  
  
    function convertToBoltItem(item) {
    const stringPrice = item.price.toString();
    const priceLen = stringPrice.length;
    return {
      image: item.image,
      desc: item.product_description,
      name: item.title,
      shopifyProductVariantReference: item.variant_id,
      shopifyProductReference: item.product_id,
      quantity: item.quantity,
      sku: item.sku,
      price: "$" + stringPrice.slice(0, priceLen - 2) + "." + stringPrice.slice(priceLen - 2),
      options: item.title,
    }
  }
  
    function convertToBoltCart(cart) {
    let newCart = {};
    newCart.items = [];
    for (var index in cart.items) {
      item = cart.items[index];
      var itemObj = convertToBoltItem(item);
      newCart.items.push(itemObj);
    }
    return newCart;
  }

    $(window).on('beforeunload', function(){
      if (inBoltCheckout) {
      	console.log("CARTRESET");
        console.log(previousCart);
        clearCart();
        addProductsToCart(previousCart);
      }
      inBoltCheckout = false
    });
  

    $(document).ready(function() {
      $(document).ajaxComplete(function(event, xhr, settings) {
        for (var i = 0; i < cartUpdateURLsProduct.length; i++) {
          if (settings && settings.url.includes(cartUpdateURLsProduct[i]) && (!settings.data || !(settings.data.includes("bolt=true")))) {
            console.log("URLHIT");
            console.log(getCurrentCart());
            previousCart = convertToBoltCart(getCurrentCart());
            console.log(previousCart)
            internalCall = false;
          }
        }
      });
      window.productLoad = loadProductPageCheckoutCart;

      $('input#Quantity-product-template').click(function() {
        console.log("CHANGED");
   		globalBoltCart.items[0].quantity = parseInt($('input#Quantity-product-template').val());
        configureCheckout();
	  });
           
      $('.single-option-radio input').on('change', function () {
        console.log($('#AddToCartText-product-template').text())
        if ($('#AddToCartText-product-template').text().includes('Sold Out')) {
          $('.bolt-checkout-button-product.bolt-multi-step-checkout').css('display', 'none');
        } else {
          $('.bolt-checkout-button-product.bolt-multi-step-checkout').css('display', 'block');
        }
        var chosen = $('.single-option-radio input:checked').val()
        console.log("Variant Changed");
        console.log(this);
        var count = 0
        $('.swatch-container').each(function () {
          window.elemVal = this.children[0].value;
          if (elemVal == chosen) {
            optionsSelectedIndex = count;
          }
          count ++;
          });
        console.log(optionsSelectedIndex);
        loadProductPageCheckoutCart()
      }); 
      
      loadProductPageCheckoutCart();
    });
  })();
